=== 22. TCSR REGISTER (PCIe PHY mode select) ===
TCSR[0x0000]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0004]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0008]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x000c]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0010]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0014]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0100]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0104]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0108]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x010c]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x0110]: 0x00000000
TCSR[0x1000]: Bus error
TCSR[0x1004]: Bus error
TCSR[0x6100]: 0x00000010
